  Fontconfig configuration is done via /etc/fonts/conf.avail and conf.d.
  Read /etc/fonts/conf.d/README for more information.

  Configuration via /etc/fonts/local.conf is still possible,

  Main systemwide configuration should be done by symlinks

  cd /etc/fonts/conf.d

	--fprod "\n/* enumerations from \"@filename@\" */" \
	--vhead "GType\n@enum_name@_get_type (void)\n{\n  static const G@Type@Value values[] =\n  {" \
	--vprod "    { @VALUENAME@, \"@VALUENAME@\", \"@valuenick@\" }," \
	--vtail "    { 0, NULL, NULL }\n  };\n" \
	--dhead "  static const Gimp@Type@Desc descs[] =\n  {" \
	--dprod "    { @VALUENAME@, @valuedesc@, @valuehelp@ }," \
	--dtail "    { 0, NULL, NULL }\n  };\n\n  static GType type = 0;\n\n  if (G_UNLIKELY (! type))\n    {\n      type = g_@type@_register_static (\"@EnumName@\", values);\n      gimp_type_set_translation_context (type, \"@enumnick@\");\n      gimp_@type@_set_value_descriptions (type, descs);\n    }\n\n  return type;\n}\n" \
	./widgets-enums.h > xgen-wec \

  dir=/tmp/gimp/pkg/gimp/usr/share/locale/$lang/LC_MESSAGES; \
  /bin/sh /tmp/gimp/src/gimp-2.8.14/install-sh -d $dir; \
  if test -r $lang.gmo; then \
    /usr/bin/install -c -m 644 $lang.gmo $dir/gimp20-python.mo; \
    echo "installing $lang.gmo as $dir/gimp20-python.mo"; \
  else \
    /usr/bin/install -c -m 644 ./$lang.gmo $dir/gimp20-python.mo; \
    echo "installing ./$lang.gmo as" \
	 "$dir/gimp20-python.mo"; \
  fi; \
  if test -r $lang.gmo.m; then \
    /usr/bin/install -c -m 644 $lang.gmo.m $dir/gimp20-python.mo.m; \
    echo "installing $lang.gmo.m as $dir/gimp20-python.mo.m"; \
  else \
    if test -r ./$lang.gmo.m ; then \
      /usr/bin/install -c -m 644 ./$lang.gmo.m \
	$dir/gimp20-python.mo.m; \
      echo "installing ./$lang.gmo.m as" \
	   "$dir/gimp20-python.mo.m"; \
    else \
      true; \
    fi; \
  fi; \
done

/bin/sh /tmp/gimp/src/gimp-2.8.14/install-sh -d /tmp/gimp/pkg/gimp/usr/share/locale
linguas="ar be bg br ca ca@valencia cs da de dz el en_CA en_GB eo es et eu fa fi fr gl gu he hr hu id is it ja km ko lt lv mk ms my nb ne nl nn pa pl pt pt_BR ro ru rw sk sl sr sr@latin sv ta tr uk vi zh_CN zh_HK zh_TW "; \
for lang in $linguas; do \
  dir=/tmp/gimp/pkg/gimp/usr/share/locale/$lang/LC_MESSAGES; \
  /bin/sh /tmp/gimp/src/gimp-2.8.14/install-sh -d $dir; \
  if test -r $lang.gmo; then \
    /usr/bin/install -c -m 644 $lang.gmo $dir/gimp20-tips.mo; \
    echo "installing $lang.gmo as $dir/gimp20-tips.mo"; \
  else \
    /usr/bin/install -c -m 644 ./$lang.gmo $dir/gimp20-tips.mo; \
    echo "installing ./$lang.gmo as" \
	 "$dir/gimp20-tips.mo"; \
  fi; \
  if test -r $lang.gmo.m; then \
    /usr/bin/install -c -m 644 $lang.gmo.m $dir/gimp20-tips.mo.m; \
    echo "installing $lang.gmo.m as $dir/gimp20-tips.mo.m"; \
  else \
    if test -r ./$lang.gmo.m ; then \
      /usr/bin/install -c -m 644 ./$lang.gmo.m \
	$dir/gimp20-tips.mo.m; \
      echo "installing ./$lang.gmo.m as" \
	   "$dir/gimp20-tips.mo.m"; \
    else \
      true; \
    fi; \
  fi; \
done
